1 # This file is a modified version of the Microsoft reference provided
   2 # to the Unicode Consortium. All of the single byte codepoints and
   3 # duplicate mappings have been commented out. This file serves as the
   4 # basis for creating the MS932 internal DoubleByte-only converter in
   5 # JDK 1.2, which in turn is the superclass of the public SJIS converter.
   6 #
   7 #    Name:     cp932 to Unicode table
   8 #    Unicode version: 2.0
   9 #    Table version: 2.00
  10 #    Table format:  Format A
  11 #    Date:          04/15/98
  12 #
  13 #    Contact:       cpxlate@microsoft.com
  14 #
  15 #    General notes: none
  16 #
  17 #    Format: Three tab-separated columns
  18 #        Column #1 is the cp932 code (in hex)
  19 #        Column #2 is the Unicode (in hex as 0xXXXX)
  20 #        Column #3 is the Unicode name (follows a comment sign, '#')
  21 #
  22 #    The entries are in cp932 order
  23 #
  24 #0x00	0x0000	#NULL
  25 #0x01	0x0001	#START OF HEADING
  26 #0x02	0x0002	#START OF TEXT
  27 #0x03	0x0003	#END OF TEXT
  28 #0x04	0x0004	#END OF TRANSMISSION
  29 #0x05	0x0005	#ENQUIRY
  30 #0x06	0x0006	#ACKNOWLEDGE
  31 #0x07	0x0007	#BELL
  32 #0x08	0x0008	#BACKSPACE
  33 #0x09	0x0009	#HORIZONTAL TABULATION
  34 #0x0A	0x000A	#LINE FEED
  35 #0x0B	0x000B	#VERTICAL TABULATION
  36 #0x0C	0x000C	#FORM FEED
  37 #0x0D	0x000D	#CARRIAGE RETURN
  38 #0x0E	0x000E	#SHIFT OUT
  39 #0x0F	0x000F	#SHIFT IN
  40 #0x10	0x0010	#DATA LINK ESCAPE
  41 #0x11	0x0011	#DEVICE CONTROL ONE
  42 #0x12	0x0012	#DEVICE CONTROL TWO
  43 #0x13	0x0013	#DEVICE CONTROL THREE
  44 #0x14	0x0014	#DEVICE CONTROL FOUR
  45 #0x15	0x0015	#NEGATIVE ACKNOWLEDGE
  46 #0x16	0x0016	#SYNCHRONOUS IDLE
  47 #0x17	0x0017	#END OF TRANSMISSION BLOCK
  48 #0x18	0x0018	#CANCEL
  49 #0x19	0x0019	#END OF MEDIUM
